1. The first image shows a gray circle.
2. The second image shows the top half of the circle shaded gray, and the bottom half remains white.
3. The third image adds blue shapes to the previously shaded region.

In this case, the shaded part of the circle remains consistent throughout the steps, while additional blue shapes are added in a meaningful pattern.

Now, looking at the options:

- **Option A**: Two blue shapes (one round, one square) at the top, along with something below.
- **Option B**: Different arrangements of shapes.
- **Option C**: Two blue shapes (one round, one square) on the left.
- **Option D**: Various shapes with a different arrangement.

Considering the pattern of shapes and the placement seen in the previous steps, the answer that continues the sequence logically appears to be **Option C**. 

Thus, the answer is: **C**.
